14 /**
15  * A collection of OSS Spark factory functions for all of Quality's runners provided in two flavours for ruleEngine, folder
16  * and expressionRunner.
17  *
18  * 1. xFactory (requires encoders for both input and the full output type)
19  * 2. xFactoryT (requires encoders for the underlying output type wrapped by Quality types)
20  *
21  * The T variants accept all spark encoders and, on later spark versions, AgnosticEncoders can also be used to specify
22  * java collections.  Not using AgnosticEncoders will typically result in cryptic messages about missing types as Java
23  * drops it's type information in generated classes.
24  *
25  * The non-T variants require using Frameless for type derivation with an import of quality.implicits._.
26  *
27  * No QueryPlan generating expressions (e.g. joins/correlated sub-queries etc.) may be used and their presence will
28  * trigger an exception.
29  *
30  * ProcessorFactory's create new instances on the basis of the compile, forceMutable and forceVarCompilation boolean
31  * parameters. Using compile = false will trigger interpreted execution of rules and fresh tree copies for each instance
32  * call.  The default compilation approach (forceMutable = false) reduces source code
33  * generation overhead for non-stateful expression trees (e.g. no monotonically_incrementing_id or unique_id or rand etc.).
34  * With forceMutable set as true a higher cost implementation based on Spark provided MutableProjections will be used,
35  * if there are issues in actual processing this option is worth trying.
36  *
37  * EXPERIMENTAL - forceVarCompilation = true uses a wholeStageCodeGen style approach for subexpressions and removes
38  * the use of InternalRow wherever possible, the default of forceVarCompilation = true uses InternalRow based processing.
39  * The compilation overhead is higher with VarCompilation, albeit typically paid once, but the runtime performance is
40  * the fastest of the options. The compilation approach however is closer to ruleRunner than WholestageCodegen and is
41  * therefor deemed supported but experimental.  It is only supported on version 3.2.1 and above.
42  *
43  * The defaults, including runner specific compilation options, are chosen for general larger volumes of data processing.
44  *
45  * In some cases the input may need a further projection, e.g. from_avro, the extraProjection function allows for this.
46  *
47  * By default the Quality optimisations are added, e.g. funRewrite.  These may be disabled vai setting
48  * enableQualityOptimisations = false.
49  */
50 object ProcessFunctions {
51 
52   /**
53    * processor for DQ rules
54    * @tparam I
55    * @return
56    */
57   def dqFactory[I: Encoder](ruleSuite: RuleSuite, compile: Boolean = true, compileEvals: Boolean = false,
58       forceRunnerEval: Boolean = false, forceMutable: Boolean = false,
59       extraProjection: DataFrame => DataFrame = identity, enableQualityOptimisations: Boolean = true,
60       forceVarCompilation: Boolean = false): ProcessorFactory[I, RuleSuiteResult] =
61     processFactory[I, RuleSuiteResult](addDataQualityF(ruleSuite, compileEvals = compileEvals,
62       forceRunnerEval = forceRunnerEval), 1, compile, forceMutable = forceMutable,
63       extraProjection = extraProjection, enableQualityOptimisations = enableQualityOptimisations,
64       forceVarCompilation = forceVarCompilation)(
65       implicitly[Encoder[I]], com.sparkutils.quality.impl.Encoders.ruleSuiteResultExpEnc
66     )
67 
68   /**
69    * processor for DQ rules returning a pair of overall RuleResult and RuleSuiteResultDetails
70    * @tparam I
71    * @return
72    */
73   def dqDetailsFactory[I: Encoder](ruleSuite: RuleSuite, compile: Boolean = true, compileEvals: Boolean = false,
74       forceRunnerEval: Boolean = false, forceMutable: Boolean = false,
75       extraProjection: DataFrame => DataFrame = identity, enableQualityOptimisations: Boolean = true,
76       forceVarCompilation: Boolean = false): ProcessorFactory[I, (RuleResult, RuleSuiteResultDetails)] = {
77     import com.sparkutils.quality.implicits._
78     val tup = TypedExpressionEncoder[(RuleResult, RuleSuiteResultDetails)]
79     processFactory[I, (RuleResult, RuleSuiteResultDetails)](addOverallResultsAndDetailsWrapperF(ruleSuite,
80       compileEvals = compileEvals, forceRunnerEval = forceRunnerEval), 2, compile, forceMutable = forceMutable,
81       extraProjection = extraProjection, enableQualityOptimisations = enableQualityOptimisations,
82       forceVarCompilation = forceVarCompilation)(
83       implicitly[Encoder[I]], tup
84     )
85   }
86 
87   private def addOverallResultsAndDetailsWrapper(dataFrame: DataFrame, rules: RuleSuite, overallResult: String = "DQ_overallResult",
88                                   resultDetails: String = "DQ_Details", compileEvals: Boolean = false,
89                                   forceRunnerEval: Boolean = false): DataFrame = {
90     val temporaryDQname: String = "DQ_TEMP_Quality"
91     addDataQuality(dataFrame, rules, temporaryDQname, compileEvals = compileEvals,
92       forceRunnerEval = forceRunnerEval).
93       selectExpr("*",s"processor_input_wrapper(account, $temporaryDQname.overallResult) as $overallResult",
94         s"ruleSuiteResultDetails(processor_input_wrapper(account, $temporaryDQname)) as $resultDetails").drop(temporaryDQname)
95   }
96 
97   private def addOverallResultsAndDetailsWrapperF(rules: RuleSuite, compileEvals: Boolean = false,
98                                    forceRunnerEval: Boolean = false): DataFrame=> DataFrame =
99     addOverallResultsAndDetailsWrapper(_, rules, compileEvals = compileEvals,
100       forceRunnerEval = forceRunnerEval)
101 
102   /**
103    * processor for DQ rules returning a pair of overall RuleResult and a LazyRuleSuiteResultDetails
104    * @tparam I
105    * @return
106    */
107   def lazyDQDetailsFactory[I: Encoder](ruleSuite: RuleSuite, compile: Boolean = true, compileEvals: Boolean = false,
108                                        forceRunnerEval: Boolean = false, forceMutable: Boolean = false,
109                                        extraProjection: DataFrame => DataFrame = identity, enableQualityOptimisations: Boolean = true,
110                                        forceVarCompilation: Boolean = false, defaultIfPassed: Option[RuleSuiteResultDetails] = None):
111           ProcessorFactory[I, (RuleResult, LazyRuleSuiteResultDetails)] = {
112     import com.sparkutils.quality.implicits._
113     implicit val rowEnc = Encoders.internalRowTypedEnc(Encoders.ruleSuiteResultDetailsTypedEnc.catalystRepr)
114 
115     val tup = TypedExpressionEncoder[(RuleResult, InternalRow)]
116     val defaultIfPassedProxy = defaultIfPassed.map(LazyRuleSuiteResultDetailsProxyImpl(_))
117 
118     val iEnc = implicitly[Encoder[I]]
119 
120     val r = processFactory[I, (RuleResult, InternalRow)](addOverallResultsAndDetailsWrapperF(ruleSuite,
121       compileEvals = compileEvals, forceRunnerEval = forceRunnerEval), 2, compile, forceMutable = forceMutable,
122       extraProjection = extraProjection, enableQualityOptimisations = enableQualityOptimisations,
123       forceVarCompilation = forceVarCompilation)(
124       implicitly[Encoder[I]], tup
125     )
126 
127     ProcessorFactoryProxy(r, (p: (RuleResult, InternalRow)) => {
128       (p._1,
129         if (p._1 == Passed)
130           defaultIfPassedProxy.getOrElse[LazyRuleSuiteResultDetails](
131             LazyRuleSuiteResultDetailsImpl(p._2)
132           ) else
133           LazyRuleSuiteResultDetailsImpl(p._2)
134       )
135     })
136   }

190   def lazyRuleEngineFactory[I: Encoder, T: Encoder](ruleSuite: RuleSuite, outputType: DataType, compile: Boolean = true,
191                                                     compileEvals: Boolean = false,
192                                                     forceRunnerEval: Boolean = false, forceTriggerEval: Boolean = false, forceMutable: Boolean = false,
193                                                     extraProjection: DataFrame => DataFrame = identity, enableQualityOptimisations: Boolean = true,
194                                                     forceVarCompilation: Boolean = false)(implicit oenc: Encoder[Option[T]]): ProcessorFactory[I, LazyRuleEngineResult[T]] = {

199     implicit val enc = TypedExpressionEncoder[(InternalRow, Option[SalientRule], Option[T])]
200 
201     val r = processFactory[I, (InternalRow, Option[SalientRule], Option[T])](ruleEngineWithStructF(ruleSuite, outputType,
202       compileEvals = compileEvals, forceRunnerEval = forceRunnerEval, forceTriggerEval = forceTriggerEval), 1, compile,
203       forceMutable = forceMutable, extraProjection = extraProjection, enableQualityOptimisations = enableQualityOptimisations,
204       forceVarCompilation = forceVarCompilation)(
205       implicitly[Encoder[I]], enc)
206 
207     ProcessorFactoryProxy(r, (p: ((InternalRow, Option[SalientRule], Option[T]))) => {
208       LazyRuleEngineResult(LazyRuleSuiteResultImpl(p._1), p._2, p._3)
209     })
210   }

423   /**
424    * processor for expressionRunner with encoding over the nested T in GeneralExpressionsResult[T].  You must supply
425    * the outputType for T
426    * *Note* you must use AgnosticEncoders in 3.4+ in order to be able to support Java collections/generics,
427    * reflection via .bean is not sufficient for java generics.
428    * @tparam I the input type
429    * @tparam T the result type of the rule engine
430    * @return
431    */
432   def expressionRunnerFactoryT[I: Encoder, T: Encoder](ruleSuite: RuleSuite, outputType: DataType,
433       compile: Boolean = true, compileEvals: Boolean = false,
434       forceRunnerEval: Boolean = false, forceMutable: Boolean = false,
435       extraProjection: DataFrame => DataFrame = identity, enableQualityOptimisations: Boolean = true,
436       forceVarCompilation: Boolean = false): ProcessorFactory[I, GeneralExpressionsResult[T]] = {
437     import com.sparkutils.quality.implicits._
438     implicit val ttyped: TypedEncoder[T] = fromNormalEncoder[T](outputType)
439     implicit val enc = TypedExpressionEncoder[GeneralExpressionsResult[T]]
